dilationW 1\n#define strideT 1\n#define strideH 1\n#define strideW 1\n\ntemplate<typename T>\nconstexpr T div_up(T a, T b) {\n    return (a + b - 1) / b;\n}\n\nconstexpr int LDS_SIZE = 32*1024;       // with 64-KB LDS, this allows occupancy=2\nconstexpr int weight_size = KD*KH*KW;   // in unit of IO_DTYPE\nconstexpr int max_input_size = LDS_SIZE/sizeof(IO_DTYPE) - (weight_size + 31)/32 *
